The nose behind this fragrance is Jacques Polge. Top notes are Orange, Sea Notes, Aldehydes and Blood Mandarin; middle notes are Pepper, Neroli and Cedar; base notes are Vanilla, Tonka Bean, White Musk, Amber, Vetiver and Elemi resin. </p><div v-pre class='fragrantica-blockquote'><p>Five years after the launch of Allure Homme, Chanel house presented Allure Homme Sport, which came as a fresher and sharper fragrance. The crystal clear beginning introduces notes of water and aldehydes. It is followed by woodsy and spicy character of the fragrance, which thanks to luminous vetiver is not oriental heavy, but light and translucent. The base is composed of sensual white musk, tonka beans and amber. It was designed in 2004 by the famous \'nose\' of Chanel house, Jacques Polge.</p></div><p class="reviewstrigger" style="font-size: smaller; color: #83a6c4">Read about this perfume in other languages: padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2266056" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="fragrantlyenhanced"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1453129"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1453129.gif" class="comments-avatar"alt="fragrantlyenhanced" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2266056ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2266056" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.79); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1453129">fragrantlyenhanced</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-30">08/30/24 12:15</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>there is a genuinely underappreciated genre of fragrances that are meant to be worn with physical activity in mind. there people who think its weird to wear a fragrance to the gym. but to me its a must. there scents that completely change the way they smell when your heart rate increases and you break a sweat. a very specific condition. you have to be very careful what you choose as the increased body heat can do weird things with the notes and turn unpleasant for everyone around you. i had that happen with the eau extreme. it doesn't mix at all with your sweat and can turn quickly into a sort of ''powdery fecal'' smell... althou i really like the eau extreme.. not for the gym... even versace pour homme which is on the cheaper side and also has performance issues. it smell great once you start but later on turned into an overdose of pool chlorine mid workout.<br />
<br />
but this one? perfect. made me feel clean and it didn't annoy me or anyone else. both don't have the performance or projection after 1-2 hours. not great for casual wear. however that's exactly what you want for a gym session. matter the fact this one. mmmm smells so fucking good once the heat reacts to it. so fresh, clean, subtle but very noticeable. masculine citrusy clean facets of neroli combined with ozonic elements on top a musky creamy airy vanilla with an ambery / citric elemi. that just sticks for the whole remainder of your work out and slightly after. ''simple'' for chanel's definition. generic? not really. perfect frag for the occasion. you don't want anything complex/lasting that you'll shower off anyways after the gym.<br />
<br />
i think everyone sort of already know what to expect from this fragrance so i don't know what to add really. i can vouch for it to be the perfect gym scent that's bit more on the pricier side. like there so many fragrances that you'd consider light but once you start to move they can turn foul real quick, this doesn't do that. it is weak by itself really. but when your core temperature rises. all the performance issues people complain about? no longer there. <br />
<br />
the question is whenever or not its worth the price just for that purpose. as a regular in the gym i think it is. i haven't found anything that did it better and i tried. maybe some of the aqua di parma line but then you're entering an even more expensive price bracket. so many compliments just in the gym. outside of that i don't see a purpose to it. it puts me in the right mood to lift some heavy ass weights!<br />
<br />
gym essential/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="2266056"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=2266056#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2265735" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; That would be me and I can say save your money on the Chanel and just get Missoni Wave. They are 90% similar with the only differences being Missoni Wave has a slightly more synthetic smell and is a bit heavier. That does mostly die out after drying down for a little while but you are left with a very close Chanel Allure Homme Sport and it actually performs quite a bit better than Chanel as well. I will also say if you’re a huge fan of this DNA like I am the best of the three is most definitely Versace Pour Homme. Also if money isn’t an issue just get all three, I own all three and have worn them all heavy and I adore all three for specific reasons but when it comes down to facts Versace is king and Missoni smells almost identical to Chanel. The reason Versace is the best of the three in this DNA is because it drops the heavier creaminess and just explodes with nothing but beautiful clean citrus with slight florals trailing behind it is the absolute best in this DNA.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2137868">EmilZakaryan924</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-28">07/28/24 14:51</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I went to the Chanel boutique to try out some of their mens fragrances. <br />
<br />
This is my 4th favorite fragrance in the Allure Homme line. Starts off citrusy, marine, woody, with a touch of vanilla in the base. Drys down to a more woody version of the opening in my opinion. Very basic but still a very nice fragrance. I still prefer Allure Homme Sport Cologne over this but this is still a nice fragrance from the line. <br />
<br />
Let's talk about performance. I got around 6 hours on my skin with a medium projection leaning on the masculine side. I recommend this for the spring and summer, and this is definitely a day time fragrance. <br />
<br />
Lastly, is it a safe blind buy? Yes it is.<br />
<br />
In conclusion: <br />
Scent: 8.5/10<br />
Longevity: 6.5/10<br />
Projection: 6.5/10<br />
<br />
Chanel Allure Homme Sport: 8/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="2232051"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=2232051#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2229895" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:1,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Aldehydes and citrus blend well to create a fresh, bright opening. As it dries the vanilla and tonka comes out which plays very well with the fresh citrus and adds musky, sweet depth. Gotten a few compliments with this. Sadly the performance isn't great and within 4 hours you'll need to respray. And after wearing this daily for months I find the opening a bit too sharp. I sampled eau extreme and it performs better but not by a lot. <br />
<br />

Versace Pour Homme is also a very good alternative for much cheaper with brighter citrus tones in place of the aldehydes although I prefer the vanilla notes of the Allure Sport.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2193469" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Whateverwhocares"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1757007"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1757007.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Whateverwhocares" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2193469ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2193469" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.85); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1757007">Whateverwhocares</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-19">06/19/24 15:56</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Ah, Chanel Allure Homme Sport. Here's a dumbreach if I've ever owned one. Easy, fun, smell-good-spray-away, all purpose summer vibe. <br />
<br />
The longevity leaves a little bit to be desired, but so it goes. And the scent doesn't dissipate, it just settles really close to the skin.<br />
<br />
This is a lot better than the Eau Extreme, Blanche, and other versions. But they've all got something to offer. Homme Sport is the best all around.<br />
<br />
Well rounded, refined and dependable. Homme Sport is an aquatic gemstone, filled with fresh-water aldehydes and sweet orange notes. This is one of those frags that overrides B/O but is best applied right out of the shower.<br />
<br />
It’s nicely blended snd the arrangement is harmonious. Has a ghostly projection. It’s in the air until it boils down into a vanilla skin scent.<br />
<br />
Smells fresh and the citrus accord only has a mild Pledge-like zest. Typically, your citrus notes will make the fragrance seem overly synthetic or cheap. Not the case here.<br />
<br />
The orange accord is not unlike what’s found in an Atelier’s Cologne or a glass of fresh orange juice; and it lasts about as long as it takes to drink said glass of juice. 🍹<br />
<br />
I really dig this scent. I use it casually and at work. In the office and outside. I’m going to experiment with ways to make it project more intensely and last longer (Molecule or ISO Super? — please DM advice).<br />
<br />
Anywho here’s a designer 🎨 banger! 🌞⛱️</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="2193469"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=2193469#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2191490" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I love the orange opening. I just wish it Iasted a little longer. There's a slight marine vibe and the vanilla as it drys works really well for a fresher scent. This is probably one of the most versatile scents. All year round, anytime, any place. Good performance too. I get around 7-8 hours with decent projection. However with all this being said I've always felt this was slightly overrated. It's just a nice versatile everyday fragrance. You'll have to pay full retail which is pretty much what most designers go for nowadays but it would be nice to able to get this on discounters because the quality is just good. Not mind blowing quality, it's just good. Chanel purists would disagree. I always preferred this to the Extreme flanker though. Edition Blanche is still my favorite. Overall it's good versatile fragrance. padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2143860" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="DrummerCat"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2115129"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2115129.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="DrummerCat" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2143860ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2143860" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2115129">DrummerCat</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-02">05/02/24 19:07</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is in my opinion a fantastic sporty and altogether edgier take on the original and tastefully done Allure Homme.   The sleek, cosmopolitan silver flask for me reflects perfectly the essence of the scent housed within.  A great Midsummer fragrance in my opinion, this is cool, silvery, and slightly woody with the moderate tang of Elemi coming through the mix.  My skin pronounces the Orange/Blood Orange/Neroli notes in the head and heart of the fragrance, beautifully blending them with the Black Pepper, Cedar and Vetiver to give it a chrome-like platinum sheen with a fougère overture.  On me, this scent is masculine and sporty with a freshness and clean stature that lasts all day and is a superb choice for the hot Summer months.  It is not like some of the other sport fragrances for me, which get quickly and unpleasantly synthetic and soapy on my skin.  The Orange and Black Pepper notes keep this fresh and distinctive, and the wear and silage is just right.  I like to wear this in the Summer when I go downtown on the weekend to visit the art museum with a girlfriend or haunt the farmer’s market to procure some fresh produce.  For me it is a youthful, great smelling fresh fragrance that one can toss into the gym bag and spritz after a workout and hit the town confidently.  This draws regular compliments from my female camp.   All around good smelling juice.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="2143860"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=2143860#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2140153" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1846690">RealTwizzy</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-13">04/13/24 07:01</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>a really nice scent, comforting and fresh (at least for me). works for every time of the year besides winter.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="2123462"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=2123462#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2122378" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2122378" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="cynogriffin"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2038695"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="cynogriffin" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Original-Penguin/Premium-Blend-38898.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.38898.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Premium Blend"title="Premium Blend"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2122378ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2122378" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.84); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2038695">cynogriffin</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-12">04/12/24 07:53</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Definitely a nice safe fresh smell that can be used pretty much anywhere and pretty much year-round, although I would lean on spring and summer mainly. Wasn't that much a fan of the opening, but it gets more interesting and attains more depth as it gets into the dry down. You definitely get the sweeter citrus on the top (I can identify the mandarin more than orange), along with the airy aldehydes. Everything in the middle is pretty prominent and the stars of the show in my opinion, the black peppery neroli and a subtle sharp woodiness from the cedar. Some subtle but effective musky amber gives it some depth on the dry down. I do like how this one develops through the day and from hour to hour, which I think is a great sign of a quality fragrance, and the more I wear it and experience the different notes and development of that depth, it definitely grows on me.<br />
<br />
Is it super unique? No, and especially for the price of this one, I think there are a lot of alternatives to consider in this DNA range. Is it interesting? It's not groundbreaking or super unique, but as far as freshies and everyday scents go, it has a good amount of development and intrigue. Definitely a crowd-pleaser and blind-buy safe (if you want to shell out the cash). Might not be your favorite scent, but will likely be one of the scents that others like best on you. If you're okay with the price for a dumb-reach, good all-arounder, people-pleaser, and safe scent, you can't really go wrong with this one in my opinion.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="2122378"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=2122378#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2122144" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2122144" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="M-as-Marin"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1202613"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1202613.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="M-as-Marin" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Oud-Wood-1826.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.1826.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Oud Wood"title="Oud Wood"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2122144ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2122144" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.78); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1202613">M-as-Marin</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-12">04/12/24 02:12</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>One thing you should know about AHS is that a 20-year gap between a release and now does many things that usually make that older fragrance smell less original. That’s how things are and how the perfume world works. So, to put it simply, AHS is not as original as it might have been ten or twenty years ago. The most important question that one should ask himself before spending that big money is, what do I want from a summer-oriented release? Do I want a slightly generic-smelling but high-quality versatile fragrance I will use, or something like Orto Parisi Bergamask, an artistic niche beast, but you’ll never finish the bottle? If you asked me ten out of ten times, I would choose AHS. That is my opinion, and I have grown from these too artistic fragrances that I rarely use.<br />
<br />
TOP NOTES<br />
AHS opens up a refreshing burst of citrus that instantly awakens the senses. I love it, and a few other citrus-oriented fragrances(designer or niche) rarely come close to it. The main note here is a juicy, photorealistic orange that is to die for, and after all this time, it still retains its original “allure.” This vibrancy is complemented by the brand’s signature note of immediately detectable aldehydes, which are done in a masculine way, as in, for example, Dior Homme Sport 2021.<br />
<br />
HEART NOTES<br />
As the fragrance settles, we are greeted by floral touches of neroli that sit below the apparent marine accord.<br />
Although I love these “sea notes” from the 2000s, they are starting to show their age, since in the last decade we have seen many more natural recreations of this accord, yet I don’t mind it when I consider the whole package. I’m glad to report that by the time the composition reaches its base notes, all is good regarding the blend, but thinner than before.<br />
<br />
BASE NOTES<br />
So, what do I get in the base? Well, that warmness from the original Allure is still here since you can detect that vanilla, along with the other dominant notes from the opening and the heart. Marine accord works especially during the hottest days of the year, but with the price of being devoid of other darker and woodies notes that used to be stronger. Finally, white musk joins the party, leaving a subtle hint of “something sexy” that sticks around long after the citruses and aldehydes fade.<br />
<br />
OVERALL <br />
It would be unfair for me to place AHS anywhere other than in the Holy Grail category. It has endured the passing trends of perfumery and will continue to be the signature fragrance of millions of men around the world. It is my favorite from the whole Allure line, and it is the one I will gladly return to in the coming years.<br />
<br />
Read the full review at scentgrail.com</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="2122144"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=2122144#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2121992" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Allure Sport</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="2075086"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=2075086#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2069528" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1642457">ninjandrew</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-15">02/15/24 10:21</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>A quick review as a comparison between this and Allure Homme Sport Eau Extreme.<br />
<br />
Eau extreme opens with more citrus than the regular, and with a bit of mint. The mint is the first to go, and orange lasts for a few hours before being replaced by tonka bean and sandalwood. <br />
<br />
Regular Allure Homme Sport also has a citrusy opening but shares this space with strong marine notes, aldehydes and vanilla. The marine notes last for a few hours slowly giving up to more vanilla and tonka bean.<br />
<br />
While I would consider both of these fragrances to belong to the sport category, I find them both a bit on the creamy side and so aren't the sportiest frags out there, though they could have their place as sporty "cool weather" fragrances. <br />
<br />
From this family, I would recommend Allure Homme Edition Blanche if you want more citrus and less cream.<br />
<br />
Both are pleasant and with good performance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="2063175"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=2063175#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2061207" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2026867" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="junkioberyoloman"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1433053"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1433053.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="junkioberyoloman" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2026867ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2026867" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.86); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1433053">junkioberyoloman</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-01-10">01/10/24 14:06</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Aquatic citrus fragrance centered around oranges. Becomes more creamy and aldehydic in the drydown.<br />
It has a beautiful sparkle of the top, that makes this refreshing and perfect for the summer. <br />
Nobody I have met has disliked this. It’s inoffensive and perfectly safe in every situation.<br />
Sweetens up in warmer weather and gets a lot of compliments.<br />
Performance is pretty good for a freshie, especially the projection.<br />
Got a really good deal on one of those refillable, twisting travel atomizers. Atomizer is great.<br />
<br />
Scent: 9/10  <br />
Projection: 8/10 <br />
Longevity: 7/10 <br />
Versatility: 8/10<br />
Price: 5/10<br />
<br />
  Overall: 7,4/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="2026867"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=2026867#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2026682" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2026682" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Benlarsen"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1365656"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1365656.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Benlarsen" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Dior/Dior-Homme-Parfum-27417.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.27417.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Dior Homme Parfum"title="Dior Homme Parfum"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2026682ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck6x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2026682" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.85); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1365656">Benlarsen</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-01-10">01/10/24 11:28</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Overall:<br />
When it comes to Chanel for men, it's hard to find a miss. When comparing this Allure Homme Sport to others in the Chanel line like Egoist or Blue de Chanel, it's apples to oranges. As for comparing it to Allure Homme Sport Eau Extreme (to me this is the most compared in the Allure lineup), this original sport scent takes the gold. This scent is sporty, yet not comparable to other sport scents because of its high quality. Citrusy and aldehydic, yet not piercing due to the softening affects that the musk and wood have. Chanel Allure Homme Sport has the ability to exist in all seasons, but thrive in warmer seasons. It also performs very well as an intimate scent. This is a scent that women seem to time-over-time love and for that it will always be in my collection.<br />
<br />
Chanel Allure Homme Sport as a "Sport" scent:<br />
This scent is indeed a sport scent while also being an outside scent, movie night scent, office scent, whatever-you-want-it-to-be scent. Many forget that for a scent to qualify as sporty, it generally has to be clean and fresh. "Clean" is most often citrus and "fresh" is aquatic. This fragrance absolutely meets this criteria and it reaches higher status by also having softness from the tonka, vanilla, wood, and musk. None of these base notes dominate the fragrance, they simply help reduce the sharpness of the citrus and the aquatic natures. Sport scents tend to be inexpensive and this scent is not that. This scent is an addicting smell for those who find themselves in the sillage of it. Both men and women find this to be a great scent so when you're at the gym it's safe, and when you're having a night in it is also safe.<br />
<br />
Allure Homme Sport vs. Eau Extreme:<br />
Imagine a gas gauge that has "empty" on the left and "full" on the right. For the sake of properly differentiating the two scents, "fresh and aquatic" will be on the left side and "soft and sweet" will be on the right. Allure Homme Sport tips the needle 85% toward the fresh and aquatic side, but not fully. Tonka and musk are there, but are not the drivers. Eau Extreme, on the other hand, has the needle tipped 85% toward the soft and sweeter side. Common notes in both are orange, tonka, and musk. The orange in Allure Homme Sport shines more than in Eau Extreme. The tonka and musk in Eau Extreme dominates the scent compared to Allure Homme Sport. The tonka alone in Eau Extreme is a beast, making it soft and sweet with a hint of freshness from the orange. Both are very different wears, but awesome. If I had the choice of which I would defer to, I would go with the original Allure Homme Sport due to the versatility it has with regard to settings. In every setting it will be positively received. Eau Extreme has always struck me as a date scent and more intimate as a scent.<br />
<br />
Allure Homme Sport positive anecdotes:<br />
I've warn Chanel Allure Homme Sport on dates, outings, interviews, weddings, etc. In chronological order I'll share the most standout moments.<br />
-2019: Being demanded throughout the entire night that I share what scent I was wearing by a woman at a local bar.<br />
-2019: I worked indoor security for a popular college bar/club and whenever I wore the scent, women would aggressively smell the spots that I sprayed. Picking up my arm (sprayed on wrists) and smelling close to my neck. I stopped wearing the scent when working because of the intense attention it brought in. <br />
-2020: My friend's girlfriend loved my scent so much that she purchased it for my friend to wear.<br />
-2020+: On all dates that I've been on since, I've rotated scents and tried others. Without doubt, Allure Homme Sport gets acknowledged and singled out. It's a single-out where the point is clear that I should just wear the scent and not cycle. Out of my collection, this scent and Blue de Chanel Parfum are the most favored and preferred.<br />
<br />
How to Wear:<br />
Application is interesting on this one. 2 sprays is what I recommend, but one could scrape by with one. The longevity is great and lasts all day. When spraying on clothing, the scent stays consistent and lasts a long time without softening or evolving much. On skin, the scent does blossom and soften after several hours. The only thing that truly changes the most from the application is the sillage. I could see respraying after 6+hours if the setting demands a stronger sillage, but if the setting is more close-quarters, respraying most likely won't be necessary. Because the scent is so balanced, having a stronger spray seems to go under the radar because of how well it's perceived.<br />
<br />
Rating: 6-10/10 (see below)<br />
I'm breaking this into two categories--what I like and what others like. For myself, I've gotten into more peculiar and unconventional scents since originally purchasing. Notes that are risky and bizarre. Megamare by Orto Parisi, Ganymede by Marc-Antoine Barrois, and Black Sea by Lorenzo Pazzaglia are my current favorites. I often wear scents by myself because what I love is not for everyone. New and interesting is what I love to discover. Does this scent hit that for me? No. To be more than honest, I call this cologne "crowd pleaser" because the only time it's worn is for others. I honestly don't even smell it anymore from wearing it so much. I would give this a 6-7/10 within my own collection. For the sake of wearing this for others, this is an 11/10. This cologne is an INCREDIBLY safe buy/blind buy and deserves to be a daily driver. I've driven this ride many times and without doubt, when I'm seeing anyone romantically, Allure Homme Sport becomes the wrist cuffing scent that I'm placed under arrest with.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="2026682"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=2026682#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2026658" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Good for office and versatile for general use. I prefer it to Eau Extreme which has proven itself to be too sickly sweet for me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="2019866"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=2019866#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2017583" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1484829">Fabean</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-01-02">01/02/24 02:56</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This stuff is super aldehydic on me. From the first spray, I get oranges and aldehydes with a tiny bit of neroli in the back. It projected really well for a few hours and then it started dying down slowly. I could still smell it in the air lightly after that tho so longevity is really good. Not a bad scent at all. padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2015979" class="cell small-2" ><div ><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="SundyPace"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1300873"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1300873.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="SundyPace" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2015979ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2015979" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.72); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1300873">SundyPace</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-12-31">12/31/23 05:19</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is better than Eau Extreme.<br />
<br />
I find Eau Extreme too creamy and too dense with its tonka bean overdose. <br />
<br />
This one is much more balanced.  It smells like creamy oranges and sea air. It's very pleasant and easy to wear. That being said, it's also a bit generic and I got bored of it overtime.<br />
<br />
Performance is decent. I once got a compliment on it 5 hours after application.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="2015979"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=2015979#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2007766" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2007766" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Scent1nel"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1231696"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="Scent1nel" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2007766ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2007766" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.71); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1231696">Scent1nel</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-12-22">12/22/23 04:51</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>What an undeniable gem this fragrance is. It took me forever to figure this one out and I snubbed it for the longest time but when I manage to wrap my nose around it, I became addicted. First of all it is simultaneously the 3rd best in the allure line(the best being Edition Blanche), and a tied 2nd. What makes it the 2nd best is it's stellar opening which I rate a 9.4/10 and tends to last up to an hour by which time it drops a little and thereafter drops quite a bit to an 8.7 in the deep dry down(after 2h+). Don't get me wrong even in the dry down it is a great fragrance, definitely collection worthy and better than most fragrances out there, I just wish there was a way to keep that opening lasting throughout the life of the fragrance. I generally do not like fragrances that change significantly across time(unless they get better with time which doesn't happen often).<br />
<br />
 It opens up with this intoxicating mix of aldehydes, sea notes, citrus(mostly orange) perfectly balanced pepper all on a bed of impeccably proportioned vanilla, tonka and amber alongside a strong dollup of musk. The opening is otherworldlybut by the hour mark we notice the aldehydes sea notes and orange die down significantly with the vanilla and tonka also oddly enough get minimised(even though they are in the base) while the pepper and musk get amped up significantly. Or maybe they are as strong as in the opening it's just everything else reduces significantly. This combination of strong musk and pepper is what probably put me off this fragrance for the longest time. It isn't bad but just did not make the cut as far as I was concerned. It's when i learned to ingore that slightly and try to look for the other notes(not gone entirely, still detectable if you focus on them) that it became more and more appealing to me in the dry down. Coupled with that mesmerising opening this became a no brainer for me with an average score around a 9/10. <br />
<br />
So here's what's on my wish list for Chanel moving forward given that they haven't put anything new out for men in 5+ years. Essentially any one(or all) of the following in descending order of importance:<br />
<br />
4. A new Allure flanker entirely.<br />
<br />
3. A new Egoiste or Pour Monsieur flanker updated slightly to modern sensibilities without losing too much of their original character.<br />
<br />
2. A reformulation of Allure Homme Sport where they manage to maintain that opening throughout the life of the fragrance. To my nose, even if they could reduce the musk a little(possibly even the pepper), dial up the vanilla aldehydes and orange slighty I can imagine them striking absolute perfection with this gem. Of course people might get pissed off with such a dramatic chane to the fragrance, so if they go with the latter perhaps release an entirely new flanker and call it Allure Homme Sport Intense(or Essentiel or Extrait or Exclusif or something to that effect). If they go with the former, that is, just make that opening(especially the first 15 min) last all throughout they don't need a new flanker just "change" the concentration as they did for EB and AHSEE to an EDP. I'm sure most people would welcome such a change as I doubt there is anyone that dislikes that brilliant opening. <br />
<br />
1. A new Chanel men's line.<br />
<br />
Jacques Polge is my favorite designer perfumer of all time so when I heard his son was taking over I was skeptical. However when I found out he is the creator of Spicebomb EDT as well as Bleu Parfum and several other gems(especially on the women's side) I realized that Chanel was in good hands. I hope he is working on one or all of the above and I hope he lives up to his father's masterful brilliance!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="2007766"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=2007766#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2004437" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It'd be perfect for a nice day in the spring or summer. This is definitely easier for younger guys to pull off than Bleu de Chanel.<br />
<br />
Overall a clean smelling and well-blended fragrance but I'd say its a little too basic for the price.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="1955264"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=1955264#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1954550" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; For that reason, the performance isn't the best, but this should be worn in the daytime during spring and summer, so the performance doesn't need to be massive. It's just a beautiful, watery, light citrus. My favorite of the allure homme line, I prefer this over AHSEE.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="1904984"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=1904984#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1903542" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1340122">nakia_lds31</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-08-16">08/16/23 08:40</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I get a prominent airy, watery, cool vibe out of this, and a minty vanilla. My nose is not picking up the citrus note at all. I don't detect the orange or mandarin. Not saying that they aren't there..other noses may pick up different notes than mine, but that is what I smell prominently. I really do like the scent for as long as it lasts, and that is the major problem I have. It's a really nice, classy, casual man's fragrance. Think white linen shirt with rolled up sleeves with matching linen trousers and attending a boat party. That's what this is. The scent just vanishes on my skin though. It's gone in 4 hours. For the price, that is abysmal and just doesn't make it a very good value.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="1903542"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=1903542#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1900965" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1900965" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="minhoEK3"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1525221"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1525221.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="minhoEK3" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1900965ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1900965" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1525221">minhoEK3</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-08-13">08/13/23 01:55</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Full circle moment for me. It was about 6 or 7 years ago, i went to department store, i tried few fragrances, i didnt know anything about fragrances. The one that striked me the most was Allure Homme Sport. I had to spray it on my shirt..i couldnt stop smelling me whole day. After about 24 hours i still could smell it on that shirt i was amazed. Before that i had some Adidas fragrances and Ferrari Scuderia Red which my brother bought me. Later i went to that Notino regularly to try some fragrances. But it was still Allure Homme Sport that i liked the most. Then some time later i found out fragrantica website and i found out that there are fragrances that smell similar to this but cheaper because i was student back then i couldnt afford it. I was thinking about Versace Pour Homme, but it was still like 50 euros. Then suddenly Missoni Wave 100ml was on sale for 25 euros + free shipping i bought it instantly. Then i started to watch youtube fragrance videos(Jeremy and then others) still with low budget but i ended up with about 7 or 8 fragrances and many many decants. I gotta say didnt use any of them maybe a few sprays as Missoni was my signature scent. Last week i sold all of them, decided to pull the trigger on Allure Homme Sport 150ml from Chanel site. <br />
Ok now to the scent. Very nice, creamy citrus in the opening, aldehydes and then tonka bean drydown which is lovely! Very similar to Missoni Wave but just like with every "clone" or "inspired by" there is always some sharp note/something a bit different etc. I have yet to come to 1:1 clone. But if you wanna AHS on budget i would say Missoni is the way however where i live price went up to 70 euro for 100ml and 60 for 50ml. <br />
Projection is quite strong for first hour/2hours then it becomes more of skin scent that lasts 4-6 hours but i dont like to say how the sillage/projection in fragrances are because it is very subjective but AHS is definately no beastmode and even Missoni can be stronger judging from initial wearing. Maybe maceration can help but i am type of person who dont like beast projecting fragrances and fill the room. <br />
It is very good signature scent, could be worn all day long every season, however i would say in winter  or cold night there are better winter fragrances to wear. Winter is slowly coming so then i might edit this review how it will perform.<br />
Is this fragrance basic,linear or "everybody on street wears it" ? Maybe....<br />
Is this fragrance overpriced? Maybe...<br />
Are there better fragrances? Maybe.. <br />
Do i like it ? Yes, i love it, it was love on first sniff :)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="1900965"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=1900965#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1900958" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;  <br />
 Similar fragrance: Montblanc's Explorer. Both Explorer and Allure Homme Sport EDT have 'fresh, citrus' images. Both smell like some shaving cream.<br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1647189">dayonee</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-08-08">08/08/23 15:34</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>AHSEE was my first Allure and love it, but a bit heavy for summer for my taste. Got the AHS to wear it in the summer but one can definitely wear this for spring/summer/fall. Got it as a backup bottle for my AHSEE since I fell in love with the overall DNA (yes, very late to the game). <br />
<br />
Fresh and creamy. More "luxurious" smelling than VPH. Blind buy and signature worthy. I'd say this and/or AHSEE are a must have in your collection. Longevity could be better but hopefully bottle maceration can help, as it did for my AHSEE (to a certain extent). LOVELY.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="1897290"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=1897290#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1894930" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I’d never buy this. It’s clean and fresh, but in a sterile, boring and synthetic-smelling way.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="1881132"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=1881132#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1880967" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1880967" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="JusttheFactsMan"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1733487"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1733487.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="JusttheFactsMan" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Montale/Infinity-81773.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.81773.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Infinity"title="Infinity"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1880967ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1880967" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1733487">JusttheFactsMan</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-07-17">07/17/23 16:32</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>#170 in my "Tour de Fragrance" The listed notes are pretty much what you expect in a "Sport" flanker, which usually, though not always (Example: Azzaro Chrome Sport) means a similar profile to the original with the addition of citrus, aromatic, green, and marine scents, an ostensibly "fresher" version of the original. <br />
<br />
So far, I've evaluated 172 scents and have considered 54 failures that I would neither purchase again nor wear if given to me. I credit the high success rate to primarily sticking with scents that have at least a 4.00 rating from several hundred people, with occasional exceptions, but that hasn't always been a reliable method to select fragrances I would like on me, and in this case definitely not. <br />
<br />
This flanker's combo of citrus and green notes completely shoves the sweet vanilla note of the original to one side, and adds a sharp, but temporary pomelo note in a sinus gouging opening. In my experience "Sport" flankers, as with many citrus-forward scents, lose that fresh citrus note soon after opening, and this is no exception, but it dries into a green/orange zest scent that doesn't work at all, and in fact I washed it off in ten minutes as it started to smell like rotted orange. Yes folks, this is a dreaded "scrubber" for me, and weak as Allure Homme is, it's at least pleasant and wearable, whereas on me this definitely is not.<br />
<br />
I didn't vote on sillage and longevity because I can't speak to whether this improves on the potency of Allure Homme, but when a fragrance this unappealing fades out it's a blessing. Some people clearly have had a different experience, and we all have our individual tastes and skin chemistry, but I'd give this one a wide birth.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="1880967"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=1880967#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1876956" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1876956" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Prague"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1292229"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1292229.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Prague" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Le-Labo/The-Noir-29-31872.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.31872.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="The Noir 29"title="The Noir 29"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1876956ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1876956" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.84); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1292229">Prague</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-07-12">07/12/23 07:49</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The standout benefit of wearing this scent is womens' reactions to smelling it. But we'll get to that.<br />
<br />
Chanel Allure Homme Sport is zingy, orangey, sweet, smooth, classy, and creamy. <br />
<br />
In my opinion it's the best, most unique of the Allure line, even more so than the OG Allure Homme.<br />
<br />
This is a smell that makes one excited. Excited in the way of heading off on a sunny holiday, parking up at the airport and smelling jet fuel in the warm air, or being at a beach party or some drinks in the park, or in the city dressed smart casual on a summer day, just doing summery things while the possibilities are endless. <br />
<br />
As soon as the warm weather comes, I start thinking about this lovely fragrance.<br />
<br />
It moves from an electrifying, aldehydic, aerosol gassy, and orangey opening, to an airy, creamy, sweet, sophisticated, and complex drydown without trying too hard or showing off its complexity in an obvious or clumsy way. Indeed, I've seen some online people sneer that it just smells like a fancy spray deodorant. And they're right. But they're also very wrong.<br />
<br />
Let's talk about female reactions to this one, and we kind of have to, being that those reactions are so extreme and so positive across the board.<br />
<br />
Allure Homme Sport Edt is the only fragrance with which I've received fairly regular unsolicited compliments from women, even unknown women, and all were along the lines of: "Wow, you smell beaaauuutiful! What IS that? It's such a sexy smell."<br />
<br />
Sure, people wear fragrances for themselves — and this is so classy and gorgeous that I feel on top of the world when I wear it but... if I need a sure-fire, no-risk winner that other people (mainly women) will love, it's this one and NO OTHER.<br />
<br />
I hear complaints about the price. The price is right on this one. It does what it does,  what no other can do, and it does it very, very well. It gets outlier RESULTS wit da laydeez when other fragrances don't... and that's got to be worth a few extra twenties of dollars.<br />
<br />
I don't like the puerile phrase "Panty-Dropper" nor do I try to review fragrances through that filter, but this really is the closest I've ever found to the mystical PD that people talk about. <br />
<br />
It works a special kind of voodoo over the fairer sex, for sure.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="1876956"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=1876956#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1870765" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1360143">morocco_mole</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-06-30">06/30/23 09:04</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>An intense crowd pleaser! Effervescent, crispy citrus, with a dry down alighting upon a pillow of soft vanilla and clean vetiver. I cannot deny the quality of this fragrance, it smells much more expensive than it is. And it ain't cheap! It takes a slight powdery turn after about an hour but shit, so does everything else on my skin ¯_(ツ)_/¯. I can't imagine someone disliking this fragrance. Smells great in the heat, but may be cloying in high humidity environments. I'd say it's pretty safe for the office but go easy on sprays. Performance is acceptable, and I get probably 4-6 hours which is great for my scent-murdering skin. Great atomizer too, fwiw.<br />
<br />
I can definitely see the comparison to Versace Signature, and I would even say they are 80-90% similar in the very early opening. For me, the Versace dries down much faster and lacks the added depth via creamy sweetness of the Chanel. I think Versace may be a better bang for your buck though, as it costs 1/3rd the price of the Chanel product and has similar performance and longevity. Like, all things held constant I think I prefer allure Homme sport but I don't think I like it three times as much as Versace Signature. Maybe I'm just a cheap bastard lmao.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="1868021"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=1868021#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1864169" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; However, Allure Homme Sport has some very distinct differences:<br />
-Less citrus<br />
-More airy/dry<br />
-Slight vanilla note, giving it a creamier/smoother vibe<br />
-Worse performance<br />
I am heartbroken about the performance on this fragrance. It smells SO fantastic but only lasts a few hours until it's barely noticeable even when I bury my face into the body part I sprayed it on. <br />
That being said, you can double-up on the sprays and it'll last a couple more hours than just one spray (per area) since the smell is so clean and inoffensive. But for the price tag, it's really just not worth it. <br />
I think the overall scent is better than Versace Pour Homme.
