padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1840644" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="RGH01"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1331188"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1331188.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="RGH01" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1840644ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1840644" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.81); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1331188">RGH01</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-05-24">05/24/23 06:11</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Allure Homme Sport is my favourite Chanel fragrance, not including the Les Exclusifs. It opens with a sharp and refreshing orange accord, backed up by invigorating aquatic notes and aldehydes, before pepper and neroli flourish in the heart to give the scent a soft yet masculine kick. <br />
<br />
The dry down is where this fragrance shines for me - the tonka bean and vanilla combine beautifully with the fresh orange and aquatic notes, to give the base an incredible smoothness. It brilliantly demonstrates that classic creamy scent profile that Chanel does so well.<br />
<br />
This scent has a strong resemblance to Versace Pour Homme which I also love. While the Versace is more affordable, the Chanel is much higher quality and smells more refined in my opinion. This is a must have for the summer for me and a staple in my collection.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="1840644"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=1840644#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1838915" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/632677">Dzarsos</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-04-28">04/28/23 20:14</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I’ll be honest, I started today thinking that I was going to be writing a pleased-as-punch review of Chanel’s “Allure Homme Sport”. I got it in the mail yesterday, after several years of putting it off for other fragrances – be they more unusual, or more cost-representative of what they actually were, in my mind (i.e., less likely to be the victim of brand-hype). Still, this is a persistent favourite amongst fragrance-type folks, so I approached today eager to give it a spin. After all, an endless stream of reviewers and community members couldn’t be wrong, right?<br />
<br />
As it turns out, however, AHS doesn’t really excite that part of me that "must review" (despite me clearly having decided to do so), because it’s something I’ve already had before, just by a different brand and in a different bottle. People have often said that AHS and Versace Pour Homme (or Versace Signature, its name isn’t particularly clear – the light blue one with the silver crest on the bottle) are similar. They will go on to say something like, “oh, but Allure Homme Sport is richer, creamier, more refined…” or some variation on that. This, I am sorry to say, is about 2% true, 98% wishful thinking.<br />
<br />
Don’t get me wrong, if you spray them side-by-side, there are noticeable differences between the two. The Versace opens a little more sharply, with a slightly harsh perfumer’s alcohol note, while the Chanel has a moderately sweeter undertone, due to the interplay of the tonka and vanilla base notes. The Versace is also a bit more aquatic and citric in feel, like a lemon being cut into at sea, while the Chanel is a milder citrus, like an orange Creamsicle on a veranda near the beach. Interestingly, “sea notes” are part of the breakdown for Allure Homme Sport, but not for the Versace – yet the Versace has a more aquatic vibe.<br />
<br />
So yes, there are differences. However, you will note that I have described them as being “more” or “less” a certain scent profile – this is because they are both shades of the same basic scent colour – slightly sweet, citrusy, aquatic blue.<br />
<br />
Here’s an interesting test for you. Spray the two side-by-side, with about 1 foot of space between them (I used a curtain), then back away about five feet. Give the scents a couple of minutes to breathe, then, slowly, start walking towards their midpoint. How close do you have to be before your olfactory perception registers two separate fragrances? At what point can you fully distinguish them from one another? <br />
<br />
If your answers were anything over “1ft” and “basically touching the surface with my nose”, respectively, you are a liar and a cad, and I challenge you to a duel.<br />
<br />
Seriously, though – the point I am making here, is that the two are essentially indistinguishable, by any reasonable metric, to anyone on the receiving end of your sillage. Unless someone practically draped over you, they are not going to be able to distinguish which of these you are wearing. So, if you wear scents for compliments, the emanation of a pleasant aura, or similarly public-minded reasons, it is more-or-less unimportant which of the two you wear – they read the same.<br />
<br />
Or, at least, they would, if not for one or two nit-picky little details.<br />
<br />
The first of these, and probably the most significant to the vast majority of fragrance buyers, is the price difference. In a moment of pure serendipity, I managed to get a hold of the Chanel for just-over-$100. This is a rare – and exceedingly low – price for a 100mL bottle, in the “full presentation” (i.e., not a tester). From the same site, Versace Pour Homme is currently selling for just over $40 for the same volume of fragrance; in fact, for just over $60, you can get a 200mL bottle, full presentation and all.<br />
<br />
And this brings us to the final issue, which is two-fold: quality and longevity. On the quality front, I am willing to admit that Allure Homme Sport edges out Versace Pour Homme – there is a smoothness in the opening that signifies a more well-rounded blending, and the Versace suffers a bit from the detectible blast of alcohol at launch. That said, twenty minutes later, I’d be hard pressed to tell you which one had the higher price tag, if I did not already know. Given the massive discrepancy, price-wise, this absolutely should not be the case.<br />
<br />
Which neatly ties into the second aspect – by hour six, or so, the Chanel is all-but vanished, just barely hanging on as a skin scent, and only detectible on clothing when pressed directly to one’s nose. The Versace? On skin, it’s about the same – but on clothing, I can still smell it up to two hours after the Chanel has dissipated, without having to burrow my face into my shirt.<br />
<br />
So, in the end, we have two scents, both quite pleasant, both quite similar, and both priced in a wildly inconsistent manner. Scent-wise, I rate them both highly – “citrusy aquatic blue” is a very appealing scent for warmer weather, and they both do it well. When I consider all the other factors, however, well…<br />
<br />
Chanel Allure Homme Sport:<br />
Scent: 8/10<br />
Other Factors: 4/10<br />
Overall: 6/10<br />
<br />
Versace Pour Homme<br />
Scent: 8/10<br />
Other Factors: 8/10<br />
Overall: 8/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="1820374"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=1820374#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1817598" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Very inoffensive &amp; FB worthy. Versatile. The opening is very musky for about 10min.<br />
I don’t like loud fragrances, so projection isn’t an issue, people will get a whiff of you walking by. Longevity could be improved though &amp; the orange amplified. A bit bland &amp; linear. A++<br />
<br />
Compared to Eau Extreme.. Extreme is not as fresh &amp; is a bit more dense. Main difference being the fantastic mint in the opening &amp; that terrible sandalwood in the dry down (‘2012-‘14). I will say however, Eau Extreme has more character, is more alluring/ seductive.<br />
Sport for daytime &amp; Extreme for evenings 🤤🤤<br />
Edit: 4/22/23<br />
AHS becomes a bit too musky/ powdery in the dry down. I actually like the deodorant spray more cause it lasts a bit longer &amp; doesn’t have that powdery base.<br />
The aftershave is very nice as well.<br />
Edit Edit 10/23/23:<br />
Today I Revisited the sample I had.. it’s changed a bit in the dry down. The powdery musk has been replaced with a gourmand tonka, orange, vanilla amber haze.<br />
I kept getting whiffs &amp; wondering where the different smell was coming from.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="1804468"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=1804468#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1803228" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1723118">sancho11</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-04-07">04/07/23 15:32</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Really good signature scent. I wore it for 5 months straight last year and it smelled great.  It didn't last as long as I would want it to though. But I sprayed a lot to counter the bad projection and longevity.  The scent doesn't blow your mind away, but it's a really good citrus and vanilla scent. I got my first complement from a girl in my age with this scent. We knew each other a little bit but still. We were at the gym and i had sprayed this scent on. And she turned around and said out loud  "Wow, what is smelling so good" or something in that kind. Then she realised it was me and she came closer to smell it on my neck. That was the moment I realised that this isn't really a boring fragrance (which I though before) But this was a really intoxicating scent.  Its creamy and fresh and really fits a guy inbetween the age of  14-40 I would say.   I can also say this. When my bottle ran out, I really missed this scent. It is quite expensive but is quite common at airports so when I'm going on vacation I will probably but it at a duty free, then it's really worth the money. <br />
<br />
One of the fragrances I would give 10/10 because of compliments, nostalgia and of course the beautiful juice. It does lack in the projection and longevity, but just spray a few more sprays and you will be good.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="1803228"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=1803228#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1800588" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/86068">Jern&ecirc; Knowles</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-03-12">03/12/23 07:34</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>1. It took me so many millennia to get to know him that I'm even ashamed of it! Ahahahahaha... As my grandmother says: it is better to hope late than to be disappointed early! In other words, so it's all right and I'm happy with this citrusy jewel from unsullied Chanel.<br />
<br />
2. Greenish perfume, critically correct and which transfers to the wearer a sensation of neatness, complete freshness and necessary softness. Its saline opening gives it a sensational coastal air, of the beginning of a cheerful summer, with a glass of a mix of tropical fruits, citrus fruits dancing and lots of sun on your face.<br />
<br />
3. I like the way in which "belatedly" unveils new nuances of its heart, for example, Pepper with its market-day spiciness in the midday sun, the burning and fresh Cedar logs, and more Neroli with its fresh, citric aroma and floral at the same time, which immediately reminds me of the similarity between Bergamot and Petitgrain.<br />
<br />
4. On my skin Allure Homme Sport takes a long time to evolve, I like that, but when it reaches its base it takes on a robust position, full of resinous, sweet touches that at no time escapes the virility it imputes since its opening. Well-built fragrance succulence, lasting over 12 hours and projecting over 8 hours, with praise!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="1781623"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=1781623#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1781080" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Was initially planning to get Eau Extreme… tested both on a strip and found Eau Extreme to be “softer / milder.”<br />
<br />
This one stood out right away… tested this one on a strip with a friend and even he agreed that this one smelt better (versus Eau Extreme). <br />
<br />
On first impression, this cologne gave me a vibe of someone that’s classy, sophisticated and well-put together. <br />
<br />
I took the strip home.. chucked it aside and even after 4 days, I got a whiff of it whenever I first entered my modest-sized bedroom. <br />
<br />
A couple of months later, I got myself a bottle and have been using it sparingly. <br />
<br />
Being a Chanel brand, it is a little bit on the pricier side.. but certainly cheaper than Eau Extreme. <br />
<br />
A versatile cologne that can be worn for any occasion and solid performance, it gets an 8.5/10 from me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="1768845"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=1768845#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1766728" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1766728" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Infevo"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1600639"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1600639.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Infevo" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1766728ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1766728" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.78); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1600639">Infevo</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-02-22">02/22/23 15:05</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This was the only one I was missing in the Allure Homme line (with the exception of Fraichissante Pour l'Ete). I tested AHS 7 years ago and always liked it but never really bothered buying it. Finally, I had to get it and compare it against Edition Blanche and AHSEE. Out of those three I think that AHS is the most versatile while still having great performance for an EdT. Compared to EB it lasts and projects much better. It may not be as potent as AHSEE, however, I can't imagine wearing Eau Extrème daily. AHS is a much easier wear and dumb reach for most situations. I also just now noticed how similar it is to Versace Pour Homme. Years ago I really went crazy with VPH and bonkers on the trigger. Went through a bottle within a couple of weeks and cannot stand it anymore. It is a great high heat scent if you don't overdo it but becomes cloying and headache inducing. AHS delivers a similar experience and serves a comparable use case. It just is sweeter and smoother. No sharpness of florals overtaking if you do overspray.<br />
<br />
Allure Homme is basically the more mature/oldschool version of AHS. It comes off more aromatic, thicker and deeper. More complex. But certainly less mass appeal. And AHS Cologne to me comes off as a more elegant zesty citrus and slightly more floral than AHS. While AHS reminds me of VPH more than AHS Cologne, I think that AHSC would be fitting much better to compete against VHP. Both are zesty citrus and very refreshing. Both share the neroli floral in the middle. But lack the sweetness and gourmandy qualities of EB/AHS.<br />
<br />
(I hope with all the abbreviations this is still somewhat readable. Sorry for being all over the place. Basically comparing AHS to five other fragrances here in two short paragraphs.)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="1766728"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=1766728#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1766642" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Never been sprayed before, a tester. Anyway, upon initial application, I get this strong, spritzy creamy orange note with a zesty amount of aldehydes. The tonka bean, vanilla and musk follow. This is no doubt a beautiful fragrance.<br />
<br />
Now, when I first tried it two days ago, it seemed powerful, then poof. Scent was gone. I got maybe 1-2 hours out of it. Or so I thought. <br />
<br />
Now, I wear it again at the third day and people are telling me that they know when I've been in the room because the room smells so good. I've noticed now that the scent trail leaves a nice tonka and vanilla bean note with the musk. Up two flights of stairs to boot. <br />
<br />
So, my bottle maybe needed to air out a little, it's also warmer outside, about 60ish versus the 40-50's that it was two days ago. <br />
<br />
The lady that told me that she could smell this stuff has a nose that knows! Believe me. So, I'm enjoying my bottle. <br />
<br />
I get anosomic about the second hour, and then the beautiful dry down comes in at about the third or fourth hour. This is a very good fragrance. So far, 8 hours and still going good. Sillage is modest after the first two hours or so, but strong beforehand. <br />
<br />
Longevity 10/10. <br />
Sillage 9/10.<br />
Price 6/10.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="1766010"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=1766010#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1763302" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1219482">jbinner88</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-02-09">02/09/23 16:39</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Chanel Allure Homme Sport is an absolutely amazing fresh scent.  Probably one of the best in my opinion.  It's tart and has a slightly vanillic and woody dry-down.  I wish the top notes lasted longer.  If you're trying to decide between Allure Homme Sport versus Allure Homme Sport Eau Extreme, I would recommend the original.  The Eau Extreme comes across more powdery and vanillic if my memory serves me well, making it smell a bit too feminine for me.  Versace Pour Homme is obviously the go-to cheaper alternative, but it lacks the slight sweet creaminess that Chanel Allure Homme Sport has in the dry-down.  The biggest deterrent for me is the price.  Too expensive with similar ones on the market, but it is Chanel.  Great scent.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="1756147"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=1756147#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1754919" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1295740">RayCashhhh</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-01-17">01/17/23 05:48</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Got a sample of this from my aunt on Christmas, Allure Homme Sport is an interesting "sporty" fragrance. Very bright, clean, citrusy opening, when I sprayed it over my aunt's house my cousin exclaimed "that smells really good"! I've seen this listed in someone's most complimented fragrances so that checks out. Neroli is the most prominent in the heart, with the pepper and cedar adding some edge to it. Neroli is hit or miss for me, it took some time for this to grow on me but it's a good fragrance. I wouldn't buy a full bottle of this, especially at retail, as there are other sport fragrances I prefer over this. Even tho it's not deemed a sporty fragrance, LV's Imagination has a similar vibe to this as well, and I'd take that over this. In all, this is good, suitable for all seasons and just about any occasion. 7.5/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="1736162"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=1736162#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1734683" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It's supposed to be a sports fragrance, but it's not. Comes out with an all out citrus bomb that smells like lemon, but there's no lemon in it. Has an aquatic note that doesn't seem to exist. A pepper note that is so faint you'd miss it and begins to transform into this almost vanilla drydown. Then when you think you have it figured out it releases a beautiful white musk, vetiver, and amber drydown. Finally when you think it's all done, that lemon note that doesn't exist bites again and performs the final magic trick. Don't know what the hell happened, but you want to see it again. I can't imagine someone not liking this. Exceptional fragrance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="176347"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=176347#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent670477" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It is the most balanced scent I have come in contact with. No one will be offended and you will get compliments across the board.<br />
<br />
It starts off with a nice citrus blast that is perfectly blended (ignore all the synthetic hoopla) and as it dries down becomes creamy, sweet and a little earthy. The only problem I have with this, is that this is no more a sports fragrance as Buffalo Chicken has Buffalo. It is a very well blended, creamy dreamscicle that develops well.<br />
<br />

The price tag is a bit high, some people recommend that the Versace Pour Homme is a better alternative considering the price. I agree to some extent, but I believe that Versace is a bit lighter and has a sportier vibe than this one. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/642559">shadowmoses</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2017-03-09">03/09/17 20:06</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>A WORD OF CAUTION! ANYONE WHO IS THINKING OF BUYING THIS READ BELOW (IT MIGHT SAVE YOUR MONEY AND HELP MAKE YOU AN INORMED DECISION)<br />
<br />
How low the mighty have fallen indeed.... I have 1005 Batch which says PRODUCTION IN JANUARY 2017. Now let me tell you this straight..... I am disappointed like anything!<br />
<br />
Six heavy sprays of this stuff and you can barely catch wafts of this after 1 hour. It lasts 5-6 hours max now. This has such piss poor projection that D and G The One EDP performs like a beast when compared to this. I applied The one edp and got whiffs of it for six hours at least. <br />
<br />
I thought maybe its olfactory fatigue or my skin chemistry that I am getting so piss poor performance with this and held myself back from writing a review. Then I made my dad wear this, 7 heavy sprays. He walked back into the house after 5 hours, he passes by me and I got nothing- NO SILAGE WHATSOEVER! I asked him if he could smell it off himself and he said I can't, only if i bury my nose on my wrist can I detect a very faint,very faint non existent smell. So my fears and doubts were confirmed.<br />
<br />
And before you go on saying that I got a fake. No sir. Ive been buying from that dept store for 5 years and it does not hold fakes. And I looked for fake bottle design vs original, saw the pics everything and mine was legit.<br />
<br />
Now it's clear. Chanel did this to allure homme the original. They reformulated it- the new formulation has the silver ring around the cap- and watered it down to nothing. They did this with the newer formulations of Bleu Edt; so why wouldn't the bastards fuck allure homme sport? They pretty much did it. I am so regretting my purchase, wasted my precious 100 dollars. Chanel shot itself in the foot with this. I am not buying anything from these buggers now.<br />
<br />
We the customers are being robbed, so that these greedy buggers can make of more money.And yes, Eau Sauvage EDT which is known for being low on projection and strength performed way better than allure homme sport's current formulation. A SHAME INDEED!<br />
<br />
Note: DO NOT BUY THE NEWER 2017 BATCHES OF ALLURE HOMME SPORT AND SAVE YOUR MONEY OTHERWISE YOU WILL REGRET YOUR DECISION. HOW LOW THE MIGHTY HAVE FALLEN INDEED......</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="607"comment_id="800570"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-607.html?ccid=800570#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent543156" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
